Rivet CMS analysis coverage

Priorities are proposed by Rivet authors here: https://gitlab.com/hepcedar/rivet/blob/master/doc/coverage/rivet-coverage-cms.rank (X=blacklist, ?=greylist, .=wanted, !=really wanted. Please feel free to suggest changes.)

Please note that analysis authors and PAG L2/L3 conveners are responsible for identifying analyses that should go into Rivet. These include all analyses that are unfolded to the particle level.

Rivet analyses exist for 81/507 papers = 16%. 70 priority analyses required.

Total number of Inspire papers scanned = 964, at 2020-01-13, Rivet version 3.0.1
